</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Confirms Long-Term Strategy and Details Opportunities to Drive Sustained Growth
at 2021 CAGNY Conference </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CHICAGO, Feb.&nbsp;16, 2021</B> &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) will today
demonstrate clear progress against its long-term strategic plan at the 2021 Consumer Analyst Group of New York (CAGNY) Conference. Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Dirk Van de Put and Chief Financial Officer Luca Zaramella will detail how the
company plans to continue to generate sustainable shareholder value. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In the third year of our strategic plan, we are better
positioned than ever,&#148; said Van de Put. &#147;We enter 2021 as winners in the market, with strong momentum and sizeable opportunities for sustained growth: We see clear potential to further grow our core as well as to expand our presence in
high-growth channels, categories, and adjacencies, setting us up to deliver on our targets in 2021 and beyond.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Positioned to Emerge Stronger
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At the conference, Van de Put will outline how Mondel&#275;z International is successfully executing its three-pillar strategy while
accelerating certain initiatives to steer the best course through <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> and to position the company to emerge stronger after the crisis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">By step-changing investment in capabilities and brand communications, as well as deepening its insights, the company is advancing its first
strategic objective to drive growth in its global and local brand portfolio and become more consumer-centric in the way it develops and markets its products. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The second strategic focus is to improve operational excellence through actions across its supply chain, which is helping the company to win
in the market and to maintain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> momentum during COVID. And finally, the third strategic pillar &#150; creating a winning growth culture &#150; is being achieved by measures such as increasing local
accountability and the promotion of an enhanced growth mindset. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Creating Shareholder Value </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Zaramella will highlight further opportunities to unlock sustained growth in revenue, profit dollars and cash flow supported by a virtuous
cycle of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">volume-led</FONT> growth, continued productivity gains, and reinvestment back into the business. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company reaffirmed its 2021 outlook, as well as its long-term annual financial targets
and capital allocation priorities, namely including: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Presentation and Materials </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Simultaneous
with the webcast for CAGNY participants, today&#146;s presentation and accompanying slides will be available in the investor section of the company&#146;s website (www.mondelezinternational.com) and will remain available on the website following the
webcast. The company is live tweeting from the event at&nbsp;www.twitter.com/MDLZ. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2020 net revenues
of approximately $27&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>OREO</I>, <I>belVita</I> and <I>LU</I> biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk</I>, <I>Milka</I> and <I>Toblerone</I> chocolate; <I>Sour
Patch Kids</I> candy and <I>Trident</I> gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit www.mondelezinternational.com or follow the company on Twitter at
www.twitter.com/MDLZ.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>End Note </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Organic Net Revenue, Adjusted EPS, Free Cash Flow and presentation of amounts at constant currency are
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. For definitions of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and how the company uses them to evaluate performance, as well as why the company is
not able to reconcile these forward-looking measures to their most directly comparable GAAP financial measures, please refer to &#147;Definitions of the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures&#148; and
&#147;Outlook&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to the company&#146;s Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> furnished with the Securities and Exchange Commission on January&nbsp;28, 2021. </P>
